If a class were to implement nsIClassInfo through\n76:  * inheritance, that code might QI to nsIClassInfo and keep the resulting\n77:  * object alive, thinking it was only keeping alive the classinfo singleton,\n78:  * but in fact keeping a whole instance of the class alive. be available\n25: ","endLine":25,"startLine":18},{"content":"80:  *\n81:  * Unless you specifically need to have a different nsIClassInfo instance for\n82:  * each instance of your class, you should
